Its graphical user interface (GUI) allows the user to easily browse and view videos, photos, podcasts, and music from a harddrive, optical disc, local network, and the internet using only a few buttons.\r\n\r\nIMPORTANT: This app performs with core functionality on Windows 10 S but some addons may not work.
